You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// pos, empty try block
public class EmptyTryBlock1 {
                public void foo() {
                    try {
                    } catch (Exception e) {
                        e.printStackTrace();
                    }
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).jjtGetNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).jjtGetNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            // Changed the condition to check if the try block has no statements (empty)
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                // Add violation only if the resources declared in try-with-resources are not named "ignored"
                ASTResourceList resourceList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class);
                for (ASTResource resource : resourceList) {
                    if (!"ignored".equals(resource.getVariableName())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后的编译错误后的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit("TryStatement");
        addRuleChainVisit("CatchClause");
        addRuleChainVisit("FinallyClause");
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { 
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
                ASTResourceList resourceList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class);
                for (ASTResource resource : resourceList) {
                    if (!"ignored".equals(resource.getName().getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            return data; 
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit("TryStatement");
        addRuleChainVisit("CatchClause");
        addRuleChainVisit("FinallyClause");
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
                ASTResourceList resourceList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class);
                for (ASTResource resource : resourceList) {
                    if (!"ignored".equals(resource.getVariableDeclaratorId().getName())) { // changed here
                        addViolation(data, node);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).findChildrenOfType(ASTStatement.class).isEmpty()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class) && !isIgnoredResource(node)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isIgnoredResource(ASTTryStatement node) {
        ASTResourceList resourceList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class);
        for (int i = 0; i < resourceList.getNumChildren(); i++) {
            ASTResource resource = resourceList.getChild(i);
            ASTVariableDeclaratorId id = resource.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
            if (id != null && !id.getImage().equals("ignored")) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }
}

        addRuleChainVisit(ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getBlockStatement().getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getBlockStatement().getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getBlockStatement().getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            for (ASTResource resource : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTResource.class)) {
                if (!resource.getImage().equals("ignored")) { // if resource name is not "ignored"
                    if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTResourceList.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTResourceList node, Object data) {
        Node sibling = node.getNthSibling(1);
        if (sibling instanceof ASTBlock && sibling.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTResourceList.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { 
            return data; 
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTResourceList node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent().getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node.getParent());
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) { // if the body of try statement is empty
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
            return data; // skip further checks for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { 
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) { // if there's only one child, it means the switch statement is empty.
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        if (node.getNumChildren() == 0 && node.isScopeBlock()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) { // if there's only one child, it means the switch statement is empty.
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 0 && node.isScopeBlock()) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 0 && node.getParent() instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) { // if there's only one child, it means the switch statement is empty.
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    // Added new override method for ASTBlock
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration) { // check if the block is used as a statement
            if(node.getNumChildren() == 0) { // check if the block is empty
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) { // check for try-with-resources
            return data; // skip check for try-with-resources
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {

        }

        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) { // if there's only one child, it means the switch statement is empty.
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {

    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3 && node.jjtGetChild(2) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, 
              ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, 
              ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, 
              ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);

    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkForEmptyBlock(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        Node block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if(block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    
    private Object checkForEmptyBlock(Node node, Object data) {
        Node block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if(block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.jjtGetChild(2) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) { 
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.jjtGetChild(2) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) { 
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    // ... other visit methods ...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        // If the foreach statement has only one child (ASTBlock) and the block is empty, report a violation
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1 && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    // other visit methods remain unchanged...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else {
            String variableName = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class).getImage();
            Node streamStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getFirstChildOfType(ASTStatement.class);
            if(streamStatement != null && !streamStatement.hasDescendantMatchingXPath(".//ASTVariableAccess[@Image='" + variableName + "']")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;

```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    // Other methods remain the same

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class)) {
            ASTBlock block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
            if(block.getNumChildren() == 0){
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTEmptyStatement.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    }

        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
