You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
```
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
```
```
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

    }

    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTElseStatement.class)) {

                addViolation(data, elseStatement);
            }

Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class,
              ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, 
              ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class); // Added ASTIfStatement here
    }

    // All the other visit methods stay the same

    // Add the following method
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        Node elseNode = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTElseStatement.class);
        if (elseNode != null && elseNode.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class,
              ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, 
              ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class); 
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        Node elseNode = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTIfStatement.ASTElseStatement.class);
        if (elseNode != null && elseNode.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    // ... other methods remain the same ...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        // Check for empty if block
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check for empty else block
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3 && node.jjtGetChild(2) instanceof ASTBlock &&
                ((ASTBlock) node.jjtGetChild(2)).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node.jjtGetChild(2));
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        if (node.hasElse() && node.getElseStatement().getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node.getElseStatement().getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class));
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
```

        return super.visit(node, data);

```
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    // ...existing code...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTElseStatement.class)) {
            ASTElseStatement elseStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTElseStatement.class);
            if (elseStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
            if (elseStatement.hasDescendantOfType(ASTIfStatement.class)) {
                return visit(elseStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTIfStatement.class), data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
```

===============================新加一个测试用例生成的checker repair_test_error_query_when_testing==========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

```
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
```

===============================新加一个测试用例生成的checker repair_test_error_query_when_testing==========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    }

    @Override

```
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    // ... other visit methods ...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getCondition() instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

    }

    @Override

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
    @Override

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    // ... all the other visit methods ...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTStatement.class)) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }
    
    // Other visit methods here...

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTBlock && node.getChild(1).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```java
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTCatchClause.class, ASTFinallyClause.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTResourceList.class)) {
            return data;
        }
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTCatchClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFinallyClause node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if(node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0){
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 2 && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```
